2em;\"><br></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">别相信成年人口里的“我没事”。<br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;\"></span></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><br></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">小孩子遇了委屈会大哭，四处求哄；</span><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">成年人会默默忍下</span><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">一切，风轻云淡。</span></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><br></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">成年后都学会了逞强，如何隐藏脆弱。</span><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">不会四处寻求安慰，不会情绪崩溃歇斯底里。</span></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><br></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><strong><span style=\"color: rgb(210, 83, 93);letter-spacing: 1px;\">因为越成熟越懂得——很多事对自己是事情，对别人来说只是故事。在这世界上，从来就没有真正的感同身受。</span></strong></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><br></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">“你看那个人抑郁的样子，真好笑。”</span></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><br></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">网易云被群嘲，已经挺长一段时间了。</span><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">各种段子表情包，都在给听歌的人贴“矫情”的标签。</span></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><br></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">聊到此事，有个朋友给我发了一张病历单。</span><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">她确诊了抑郁症，长期都在服药。</span><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">但她现在，已经连在网上倾诉都不敢了。</span></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><br></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">“之前我会去写一些自己的近况，心里话。</span><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">但后来嘲讽的声音多了，有人说我骗赞，说我矫情</span><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">。</span><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">我就把账号注销了，反正也没谁能帮我走出黑暗。</span><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">”</span></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\"></span></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><br></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><img class=\"rich_pages\" data-backh=\"178\" data-backw=\"495\" data-croporisrc=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/3GQek52mKtU7cIY41GVmfYTXeycMqicXkbsUHvINnQ4ZgKaKe6l3xybtmNgCVz5MfJf237ck0QWXTFmGaMfxPJQ/640?wx_fmt=jpeg\" data-cropx1=\"25.411764705882355\" data-cropx2=\"1073.6470588235295\" data-cropy1=\"103.76470588235294\" data-cropy2=\"480.70588235294116\" data-ratio=\"0.3597328244274809\" data-s=\"300,640\" 600px\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/eiccNfic7OE9KvaMQPUln4TnsVoJVpUzzJibNaEtCHZypDVxBapicVWOicSMon3geNSKOoCrLb4tOy6moGQYw1cRbUQ/640?wx_fmt=jpeg\"></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><br></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">每个人，总</span><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">有些话不适合说给任何人听，只适合烂在</span><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">心里。</span><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">生活的窘迫，工作的失意，爱的惶惶不可终日......</span></section><p><br></p><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">前段时间在餐厅，见到了一位老朋友。</span><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">和她聊起才知道，她已经离婚半年了。</span><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">我很诧异，因为她没在朋友圈提起过，也没脆弱过。</span></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><br></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">那天下午我才知道，眼前的这个女人有多强大。</span><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">丈夫当初去外地工作，她一个人在家带孩子。</span><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">送娃上学，忙上忙下，洗衣做饭，自己还要开店。</span></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><br></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">有次孩子晚上发高烧，她自己开着车送到医院照顾。</span><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">没床位了，她就在过道陪着孩子打针，一整晚没睡后她也发烧了。</span><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">最窘迫的是，她只能拜托护士帮忙看住孩子，自己捂着滚烫的额头去窗口付钱。</span></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><br></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">我说，你肯定心里很苦，但没见你提起过。</span><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">她笑了一下：</span><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">“谁都不容易，有什么好提起的呢？</span><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">”</span></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><br></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">我知道很多人，以往的崩溃都是号啕大哭，到处诉说。</span><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">现在的崩溃大抵就是低头沉默，然后笑一笑告诉自己没什么</span><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">。</span></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><br></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">过年那段时间，我</span><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">留意到</span><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">一个</span><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">女读者的微博</span><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">。</span><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">不幸的是，她的父亲去世了。</span><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">她今年23岁，人生才刚刚开始，身后的臂膀却没了。</span></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><br></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">这几个月，她一直在自己的小空间里，不断和父亲隔空对话。</span></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\"></span></section><blockquote class=\"js_blockquote_wrap\" data-type=\"2\" data-url=\"\" data-author-name=\"\" data-content-utf8-length=\"106\" data-source-title=\"\"><section class=\"js_blockquote_digest\"><section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">“我梦到我做饭，做了丸子，你和我说好吃，我真想天天给你做饭。</span><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">”</span></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><br></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">“爸我毕业了，优秀毕业生，你肯定会很开心的。”</span></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><br></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">“我梦到我带着男朋友去见你，你笑着，感觉还挺满意。”</span></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><br></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">“真希望你像无数次那样，在门口接我，等我一起回家。”</span></section></section></section></blockquote><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><br></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">后来我和这个姑娘联系上了，点开朋友圈，却是一片空白。</span><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">没有倾诉，没有难过，没有任何悲伤流露。</span></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\"><br></span></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">我安慰她，</span><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">成长的日子总要经历孤独的。</span><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">她的头像显示“正在输入中”，隔了很久，她问我：</span><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">“</span><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">一切都会过去的，对吗？</span><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">”</span></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><br></section><p style=\"text-align: center;\"><img class=\"rich_pages\" data-ratio=\"0.75703125\" data-s=\"300,640\" data-type=\"jpeg\" data-w=\"1280\" style=\"max-width: 600px\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/eiccNfic7OE9LZPK5Uuo5Fj8lG9m8lTchCyPZh3ZQ6VZlPC7NJoMjicYeG6dt2rH7UdwMbJQUzGUE2EKKsYDKptibg/640?wx_fmt=jpeg\"></p><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\"><br></span></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">人生还有眼泪也冲刷不干净的巨大悲伤。</span><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">生活教会我们，如何做一个不动声色的大人。</span><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">挺过来的，人生就会豁然开朗；</span><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">挺不过来的，时间也会教会你与它们握手言和。</span></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\"></span></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><br></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">前段时间，有个做影院的朋友挺不容易。</span><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">几个月没有收入，还得给员工发工资，维持运转。</span><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">他信用卡都套光了，亲戚能借的借，想办法凑。</span><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">半价卖电影周边，在门口卖爆米花，这些他都做了。</span></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><br></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">尽管很难，但他从来没有抱怨过一次，对朋友吐苦水。</span><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">直到最近影院开了，他的眉头终于舒展开来。</span><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">卖出电影票的那天，他开心地发了朋友圈：</span><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">“谢谢大家，有机会我请你们看电影。</span><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">”</span></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><br></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">他终于也敢告诉我们，那段时间他掉了多少头发，失了多少眠。</span></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\"><br></span></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\"></span><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">“我不是不脆弱，只是不想让你们感到世界的不易。</span><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">”</span></section><p><br></p><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">挺感慨的，人生真的是一个孤立无援的过程。</span><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">我也相信，那些你尝尽的世间冷漠，走过的漆黑道路。</span><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">你熬过来了，就一定会有转机。</span><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">辗转难眠过后</span><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">，一定会</span><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">苦</span><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">尽甘来的。</span></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><br></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><strong><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(210, 83, 93);\">告诉自己：我很好，以后一定会更好。</span></strong></section><p style=\"line-height: 2em;margin-left: 0px;margin-right: 0px;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\"><br></span></p><h1 style=\"white-space: normal;max-width: 100%;visibility: visible;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\" style=\"max-width: 100%;visibility: style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;\">“每一位返校的京外学生都要做核酸检测。”</strong></span>北京化工大学党委副书记宋来新透露，核酸检测费用由学校承担。</span></p><p style=\"max-width: !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">李奕对此做出解释，考虑到目前全国的整体防疫形势，特别是还有部分地区存在个别的疫情反弹情况，这项要求是从学校安全和整体防疫角度考虑。</span></p><p style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 2em;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br></p><p style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 2em;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">李奕说，不同学校返校节奏和生源情况不同，所以核酸检测如何进行由各校自行安排，灵活处理。<span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(171, 25, 66);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;\">如学生所在地不具备核酸检测条件，可先持健康“绿码”返京，入住学校健康观察点，待核酸检测阴性后转入正常学习生活。</strong></span></span></p><p style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 2em;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br></p><p style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 2em;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">据北京头条报道，8月14日下午，北京市教委举行2020年北京市各级各类学校秋季开学工作新闻发布会。北京市委教育工委宣教处处长寇红江介绍，高校学生返京核酸检测费用，由学校支付。</span></p><p style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 2em;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br></p><p style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;white-space: normal;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif rgb center border-box break-word><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\"><strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 28px;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">2</span></strong></span></p><hr style=\"max-width: 100%;white-space: normal;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif center rgb border-box break-word><p style=\"max-width: 100%;text-align: center;line-height: 2em;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(0, 122, 170);font-size: 20px;letter-spacing: 1px;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;\">高校“相对封闭”管理</strong></span></p><p style=\"max-width: 100%;text-align: center;line-height: 2em;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(0, 122, 170);font-size: 20px;letter-spacing: 1px;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;\">“十一”假期能否离校？</strong></span></p><p style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 2em;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\"><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></span></p><p style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 2em;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\"><strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(171, 25, 66);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;\">新学期开学，高校不再全封闭管理，而是相对封闭管理。</span></strong>李奕说，就目前而言，如果学生想出校和同学聚餐，去健身房健身等，还是需要谨慎一些，如果能在校内完成的活动还是尽量在校园内完成。</span></p><p style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 2em;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br></p><p style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 2em;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\"><strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(171, 25, 66);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;\">“非必要不出校”，“必要”的标准是什么？</span></strong>北京化工大学党委副书记宋来新举例，比如研究生、导师要和校外单位进行科研合作；学生外出就医；研究生助教助研助管，需要往返不同校区；外地学生父母来京看望孩子……这些情况经申请后都可以获得批准。“申请程序都是线上进行，很方便，很快捷。”</span></p><p style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 2em;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br></p><p style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 2em;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">李奕表示，<strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(171, 25, 66);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;\">会随时动态调整防疫措施和具体的工作要求。</span></strong>按照目前的安排，9月7日左右将完成大部分学生的返校工作，之后校园运行三周，再结合当时全国和北京的疫情发展情况，确定国庆中秋假期的具体工作要求。</span></p><p style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 2em;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br></p><p style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;white-space: normal;font-family: center;line-height: 2em;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 20px;color: rgb(0, 122, 170);letter-spacing: 1px;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;\">军训正常进行</strong></span></p><p style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 2em;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br></p><p style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 2em;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">李奕表示，在整体的疫情防控常态化过程中，学生群体和学校环境还是有其特殊性的，因为学生们要聚集在一起学习、生活，所以相应的防控措施应该比社会的其他群体更严格一些。<span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(171, 25, 66);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;\">此次开学，大、中、小学师生员工在校期间坚持佩戴口罩。</strong></span></span></p><p style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 2em;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br></p><p style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 2em;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">今年高校迎新，家长送新生，只能送到校门口，不能入校。“不让家长送学生入学，也是希望减少风险，希望家长们理解和配合。”李奕说。</span></p><p style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 2em;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br></p><p style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 2em;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">关于军训，他表示，大学生军训由各校确定，能满足防疫需求的，可以正常进行。<br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></span></p><p !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 2em;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);font-size: 17px;letter-spacing: 1px;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;\">第一，来自中高风险地区的学生，在返校前要实行自行或者集中的14天医学观察，7天内核酸检测阴性才可以返校。</strong>根据最新发布、修订后的《秋冬季新冠肺炎疫情防控技术方案(更新版)》，<strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">从低风险地区返校的学生，返校之前不需要进行隔离，但沿途要做好防护，入校后要严格按照校园疫情防控要求做好各项工作。</strong></span></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 2em;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 2em;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);font-size: 17px;letter-spacing: 1px;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">第二，对高校来讲，如果所有的学生在一个时间都回到校园，报到就是一个问题。</strong>如果错开一两天，每天的人数不至于有那么多，这对于学校开学的有序进行也是非常必要的。</span></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 2em;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 17px;letter-spacing: 1px;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">另外，对每一个学校而言，<strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">人员密度过大，可能会带来更大的风险，所以学校内部错峰也是有必要的。</strong></span></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 2em;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;text-align: center;line-height: 2em;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(192, 0, 0);font-size: 17px;letter-spacing: 1px;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">把好校门不意味着学校完全封闭</strong></span></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 2em;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 2em;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);font-size: 17px;letter-spacing: 1px;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">王登峰：</strong><strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">把好校门关和封闭式管理是两个概念，封闭式管理是学生进入校园后，没有极特殊情况不允许离开校园。严格把控好校门，就是要确保每一个进入校园的人是健康的，所以进出校门的老师和学生都要查验身份证件，同时要查验体温。</strong></span></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 2em;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 2em;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);font-size: 17px;letter-spacing: 1px;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">如果离开校园，去什么地方，行动轨迹要非常明确，要报告给相关部门。因此从校门管控来讲，没有必要不出校门，如果有事情，有工作要做，出校门也是可以的。</span></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 2em;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;text-align: center;line-height: 2em;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(192, 0, 0);font-size: 17px;letter-spacing: 1px;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">“十一”放假大学生能不能离校？</strong></span></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 2em;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 2em;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);font-size: 17px;letter-spacing: 1px;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">王登峰：</strong>原则上应由各地各校自行制定相关的一些规定。实际上可以考虑，如果一个大学生“十一”假期要回家，或者是到外地去旅游，<strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">那么他回来的时候，其实跟秋季学期刚开学时候的要求是一样的，所以这件事情应该还是由各校自己来决定。</strong></span></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 2em;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br></section></section></section></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><br></section><p style=\"white-space: normal;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;letter-spacing: 0.544px;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif rgb border-box break-word><span
